## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task involves modeling the population growth rate dP/dt as a function of time t and current population P. This is a classic population dynamics problem where growth rate depends on population size, potentially with density-dependent feedback, Allee effects, or time-varying parameters.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- {'name': 'Malthusian/exponential growth', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P', 'scenario': 'Unlimited exponential growth, rate proportional to population size'}
- {'name': 'Logistic growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P)', 'scenario': 'Density-dependent growth with carrying capacity'}
- {'name': 'Gompertz growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P)', 'scenario': 'Growth rate decelerates logarithmically as population approaches carrying capacity'}
- {'name': 'Theta-logistic growth', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2)', 'scenario': 'Generalized logistic with nonlinear density dependence'}
- {'name': 'Logistic with Allee effect', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) * (1 - c2 * P)', 'scenario': 'Strong Allee effect where growth is negative below a critical population threshold'}
- {'name': 'Richards growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) / c2', 'scenario': 'Flexible asymmetric sigmoidal growth model'}
- {'name': 'Von Bertalanffy-type growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P', 'scenario': 'Growth as balance between anabolic (power-law) and catabolic (linear) processes'}
- {'name': 'Power-law growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P**c1', 'scenario': 'Generalized density-dependent growth with fractional scaling'}
- {'name': 'Harvesting/mortality logistic', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 * P', 'scenario': 'Logistic growth with constant per-capita harvesting or mortality'}
- {'name': 'Time-dependent exponential growth', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(c1 * t)', 'scenario': 'Growth rate with time-varying intrinsic rate (e.g., seasonal or environmental change)'}
- {'name': 'Beverton-Holt continuous analog', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) - c2 * P', 'scenario': 'Density-dependent recruitment with constant mortality'}
- {'name': 'Polynomial density dependence', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3', 'scenario': 'Higher-order density-dependent effects including cubic terms'}

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Density-dependent feedback → multiplicative factor (1 - c*P) or (1 - (c*P)**n) modulating growth
- Allee effect (positive density dependence at low P) → additional multiplicative factor (P - c) creating a growth minimum at small P
- Carrying capacity behavior → growth rate crosses zero at a specific P value, suggesting factored polynomial in P
- Gompertz-type deceleration → logarithmic terms log(c/P) indicating asymmetric approach to equilibrium
- Metabolic scaling in growth → power-law terms P**c with fractional exponents (e.g., 2/3 or 3/4 from allometric scaling)
- Time-varying environment → multiplicative or additive functions of t (e.g., sinusoidal c0*sin(c1*t) or exponential in t) modifying intrinsic growth rate
- Equilibrium structure → dP_dt should be zero at specific P values; factor structure P*(c0 + c1*P + ...) reveals equilibria
- Competition/cooperation balance → opposing sign terms in P (positive low-order, negative high-order) indicating resource limitation at high density

I need to analyze the Ground Truth (GT) expression and compare it with each candidate.

## GT Analysis

The GT numerical expression is:
```
0.1699888096710614*(-1 + P/1.0472843670254641)*(1 - P/10.210545156320043)*P 
+ 0.1699888096710614*(1 - P/10.210545156320043)*P 
+ 0.1699888096710614*(1 - exp(-0.09709294493863778*P))*P
```

Let me simplify. Let me denote α = 0.1699888096710614, a = 1.0472843670254641, b = 10.210545156320043, β = 0.09709294493863778.

GT = α*(-1 + P/a)*(1 - P/b)*P + α*(1 - P/b)*P + α*(1 - exp(-β*P))*P

First two terms: factor out α*(1 - P/b)*P:
= α*(1 - P/b)*P * [(-1 + P/a) + 1] + α*(1 - exp(-β*P))*P
= α*(1 - P/b)*P * (P/a) + α*(1 - exp(-β*P))*P
= (α/a)*(1 - P/b)*P² + α*P - α*P*exp(-β*P)
= (α/a)*P² - (α/(a*b))*P³ + α*P - α*P*exp(-β*P)

So GT = -(α/(ab))*P³ + (α/a)*P² + α*P - α*P*exp(-β*P)

Let me compute constants:
- α/(ab) = 0.16999/(1.04728*10.2105) ≈ 0.01589
- α/a = 0.16999/1.04728 ≈ 0.16228
- α = 0.16999
- α*β = 0.16999*0.09709 ≈ 0.01651

So GT = -0.01589*P³ + 0.16228*P² + 0.16999*P - 0.16999*P*exp(-0.09709*P)

The key structural elements are:
- A cubic polynomial in P: c₁P³ + c₂P² + c₃P
- An exponential term: -c₄*P*exp(-β*P)

This means the GT has the form: **polynomial in P + P*exp(linear in P)**

Now let me check candidates systematically. I need candidates that can produce a cubic polynomial in P plus a term of the form P*exp(cP).

### Candidate 1:
`(P**3*c0 + P**2*c1 + P*c2 + c3*(P + c4)*log(c5*exp(P*c6) + 1) + c7)/(P + c4)`

The log(c5*exp(P*c6) + 1) is a softplus function. For large P*c6, this ≈ P*c6 + log(c5), but we can't use approximations. The GT has exp(-βP), not log(exp(...)). These are fundamentally different basis functions.

Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 2:
`(P**3*c0 + P**2*c1*(P + c2)*exp(P*c3) + P**2*c4 + P*c5 + c6)/(P + c2)`

This has P²*(P+c2)*exp(Pc3)/(P+c2) = P²*exp(Pc3) plus polynomial/(P+c2). So it gives polynomial + P²*exp(Pc3). GT needs P*exp(cP), not P²*exp(cP). These are different basis functions.

Wait, but if we can set constants freely... The candidate gives:
= (P³c0 + P²c4 + Pc5 + c6)/(P+c2) + P²*exp(Pc3)

The rational part (P³c0 + P²c4 + Pc5 + c6)/(P+c2) can be a quadratic polynomial plus remainder. But we need P*exp(cP), not P²*exp(cP). Can't match.

Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]

`(P*(P**2*c0 + P*c1 + c2) + c3*(P + c4)*log(c5*exp(P*c6) + 1))/(P + c4)`

= P*(P²c0+Pc1+c2)/(P+c4) + c3*log(c5*exp(Pc6)+1)

The softplus function log(c5*exp(Pc6)+1) is NOT equivalent to P*exp(cP). Different basis functions.

Candidate 70 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 71:
`(P*(c0*(P*c1 + 1) + c2*log(c3*Abs(P) + 1))*(c4*t + c5) + c6*t + c7)/(c4*t + c5)`

Setting c6=0, c7=0: = P*(c0(Pc1+1) + c2*log(c3P+1)). Has P*log, not P*exp.

Candidate 71 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 72:
`P*(c0*(P*c1 + 1) + c2*log(c3*Abs(P) + 1)) + c4*log(c5*exp(P*c6) + 1)`

For P ≥ 0: = c0c1P² + c0P + c2*P*log(c3P+1) + c4*log(c5*exp(c6P)+1)

Has P*log and softplus. Not P*exp.

Candidate 72 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 73:
`P*(c0*(P*c1 + 1) + c2*log(c3*Abs(P) + 1)) + c4*exp(P**2*c5)`

Has P*log and exp(P²). Not P*exp(cP).

Candidate 73 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 74:
`P*(c0*(P*c1 + 1) + c2*log(c3*Abs(P) + 1)) + c4*exp(P*c5)`

= c0c1P² + c0P + c2*P*log(c3P+1) + c4*exp(c5P)

Has P*log and exp. GT needs P*exp and cubic. Different.

Candidate 74 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 75:
`P*(c0*(P*c1 + 1) + c2*log(c3*Abs(P) + 1)) + c4`

Has P*log. No exp.

Candidate 75 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 76:
Has sin(t) dependence and sin(log(...)). No P*exp.

Candidate 76 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 77:
`P*(c0*(P*c1 + 1) + c2*log(c3*Abs(P) + 1)) + c4*exp(c5*sin(P*c6 + c7))`

Has P*log and exp(sin(...)). Not matching.

Candidate 77 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 78:
`P**2*c0 + P*c1 + c2 + c3*log(P**2*c4 + 1)`

Quadratic + log(P²+1). No exp.

Candidate 78 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 79:
`(P**3*c0 + P**2*c1 + P*c2*(P + c3)*(P*c4 + 1)*sin(c5*t + c6) + P*c7 + c8)/(P + c3)`

Setting c2=0 eliminates sin term: = (P³c0 + P²c1 + Pc7 + c8)/(P+c3). Rational function, no exp.

Candidate 79 verdict: [NO MATCH]

## Summary

None of the candidates can produce the required structure of cubic polynomial + P*exp(cP) that the GT demands.
